Overall, the hotel as a whole meets the configuration of this level and this price, good reviews!

posted:Posted July 14, 2023
msg:First of all, the hotel put a spa card in the room card paper bag when checking in. This is a kind of bundled sales, and I have every reason to suspect that the hotel and the recommended spa have improper transactions.
Secondly, Beijing Fengda Hotel claims to be a luxury hotel, but during my check-in process, I found that they aimed to control expenses. This business model made me very disappointed with this hotel. This so-called luxury hotel charges for even the basic facilities. Imagine that when you are focused on work or tired from traveling, you need to drink a refreshing bottle of Coke or Sprite in your room to relax. However, in this hotel, Coke and Sprite are hidden in the mini refrigerator. Other drinks in the same refrigerator have price tags, but Coke Sprite is not posted. The charge is only informed after use and it is much higher than the market price. This is absolutely disrespect to customer needs
Heavy.
In the end, as I forgot to bring laundry supplies, I saw that there was an extra charge for washing powder. What kind of service attitude is this? Why would a customer have to pay for basic cleaning supplies in a luxury hotel? Not only is this uncomfortable, it spoils the overall impression of the hotel. All in all, Beijing Fengda Hotel's charging policy is extremely harsh, with no regard for customers' needs and experiences. I am extremely disappointed with this business model.
Just before staying at this hotel, I stayed at another luxury hotel nearby,
Drinks are free in the fridge. If you want to enjoy the real luxury body
experience, I suggest you stay away from Beijing Fengda International Hotel and look for other options
